< review>
I highly recommend the Bagelry- I stopped here to buy a dozen bagels for a work staff meeting and had such a pleasant experience. I was in a hurry and not having called in my order I did not expect it to be that fast, but it was! Very reasonable price and delicious fresh bagels -my team loved them. Thank you for your fantastic customer service! It is so refreshing to see someone genuinely care and I hope your business thrives!</review>

1609865817748< /Date>
<rate>5</rate>< Text>
First thing to note right now is that they're thankfully still open and running business as usual, however they're just not offering in-house dining just yet. You can order over the phone or walk in for takeout.

The bagels all look heavenly, along with their fresh juices, homemade cream cheese spreads, teas and vietnamese coffees. We ordered 2 sandwiches from their list of most popular options. Lox was my go-to of course and it absolutely didn't disappoint. The number of capers on it was a bit of overkill in my opinion, but it was great nonetheless. My fiance ordered the turkey, bacon, cheese and tomato on a jalapeno bagel. I had to have a bite because I can't turn my head from all things jalapeno. So so good!

We wanted some souvenirs to-go, so we obviously ordered half a dozen bagels, specialty cream cheese, and a vietnamese coffee for the road. This consisted of 3 gourmet bagels, hawaiian, sundried tomato, and spinach parmesan bagels paired with an 8 oz. container of homemade garlic herb cream cheese spread.

I actually dropped my vietnamese coffee on the floor on the way out because I'm a huge klutz and went to clean it up but the lovely employees (I'm thinking the owner is the one who actually was interacting with us-- VERY friendly man) said to not worry about it. He mopped it up and poured me a fresh iced vietnamese coffee which I was very thankful for. Great hospitality and a kind attitude goes a very long way in the food industry. If your personality is beautiful and contagious, then that's a reason to come back in itself.

All in all... The bagels were delicious. Homemade cream cheese is AMAZING. Vietnamese coffee is strong how I like it and I'm going to be hyped for the next couple of hours because of it, LOL. Pricing is just right. They're in a prime location right off a main street and I hope they're here for a long time! Happy belated 1 year, The Bagelry!</Text>

< review>
The bagels were alright. Just alright. Big, size which is cool, filling. However, the flavor left a lot to be desired. We ordered a variety of sweet and savory but they all were rather plain tasting. Particularly, the cinnamon raisin bagels barely tasted of cinnamon. All of them had a garlicky taste, as if the slicer or toaster had not been cleaned from the previous bagel. Overall, it was okay. Would we go back? Probably not.</review>

The owner gave us a lovely walk-through of the menu, which was a nice personal touch. My Nova Classic came open faced, and that's not necessarily my preference, but the components were excellent. Make sure to ask for your bagel toasted if you order it with cream cheese, it isn't standard. The eggs in the breakfast sammies come out at about a million degrees, so be careful! The milk tea with boba was solid.< /review>

<text>I've had the absolute worse experience at this store compared to all other Target locations in the Bay area. First of all if you want something that's locked up (like a phone) you have to literally walk through the store and find someone to help you. Don't try asking up front because they will say "we'll send somebody back there" and then 30 minutes later nobody has shown up. You might have to ask every employee in the store 3 times before somebody even bothers to grab the keys to unlock the electronics. Every other Target I've been to has at LEAST one person deticated to just the electronics department.
Okay now on to the next issue. Returns, you can't return anything at this store that hasn't been purchased here. So usually if I buy an item from Bay Fair Target I can return it to any other one, I.e. San Francisco or the Target on University Ave in Berkeley. But this Target claims to be a "express store" (it certainly isn't living up to its name because I shouldn't have to wait for 30 minutes to get something unlocked).
Now usually prepaid phones can be returned for a full refund for any Target as long as you have the receipt and (depending on location) ID. Well I bought a prepaid phone (never activated it) opened it(never before had an issue returning opened prepaid phones at any Target except this one). Then when it was a almost unusable device I figured Id just returned it, same day, manufacturer defect not my fault at all. Then they said oh "no refunds on prepaid phones" I had a receipt with the date saying return by and it was dated for April 20. They refused to refund it. In the end I had to go around and get it refunded at the Target on University Ave. They made an exception because normally they are not supposed to because of it being bought at a Target express location.
All in all its been a very terrible experience at this location on multiple occasions. The people even questioned why I bought the phone in cash. If I want to buy a 20 dollar phone with a 20 dollar bill I'm perfectly entitled to. It's a free country and the 20 dollar bill is legal tender the last time I checked.
They treat everyone like some criminal for not using a card. (What if my card isn't working huh, what if I'm waiting for a replacement because it got demagnetized). The rude looks I got are not just because I paid cash but also because I had to find an employee to open the electronics cabinet and after waiting 30 minutes I walked through the store asking all the employees. Well if I didn't I'd probably still be waiting there right now 30 hours later. They lucky I wrote this review a day later after thinking it through because I have some choice words I really want to add right now.
All in all don't shop here. Save yourself the trouble and go 1/2 a mile to the Target on University Ave. The people there are actually helpful and ask if they can help you find stuff. Oh and there's always someone at electronics department<//text>< Pics>

< review>
I've been a member her for well over 10 years and I'm not one to normally complain publicly, but I'm pretty frustrated with this place as of late.

Over the last few years the quality of this has diminished. Machines hardly get fixed and always seem to break, the cardio equipment is always down or malfunctioning and half the dumbbells are either broken or completely missing. There was even a time frame where the bathroom door stall was missing a lock for over a week. Benches have been left broken for weeks and there are many simple things that go uncared for.

Many of the bars for Olympic lifts are completely bent to the point where they really should be changed out, floor mats are damaged etc..

Currently they remodeling and the place is a mess, lots of things have been moved or unavailable, one in particular being the cage for Olympic lifts which was probably the best thing about this place. This gym has been long overdue for a remodel for many years, I am just hoping that it actually gets better and not worse.

Some of the staff here is friendly and polite while others are not. The gym does offer some machines i really do like as they are more old school and I feel work better. My feelings have been quiet mixed about this place as it has been the only gym I've felt like I can always get a good workout, but as of late its all just been frustration. Not sure if this will remain my gym.

Heads up new members always get nice deals for year to year contracts while long term members don't share the same benefit, which has always seemed odd to me.

Anyways, I tried make this as unbias as possible. So maybe take what I say with a grain of salt, but I wouldn't be the first one to complain about these issue.</review>

The trainer will speak with you about fitness goals & review pricing for personal session trainings & complete a body analysis. This is not done in private & anyone in the office/around the cage is aware of your height, weight, & body classifications. I signed up for the VIP membership (49.99 per month) & personal training sessions 2x per week (400 per month). After signing up for sessions I went to my first workout, two treadmills and one stationary bike were broken. I notified the front desk & was treated very rudely. Initially I enjoyed the personal training, but found that the training regime was not for me. This gym is focused on bodybuilding/CrossFit style training. If you are seeking training that involves Pilates, yoga, etc. this is NOT the place for you. The gym does not offer space for mat exercises, except for the cage (and you have to be signed up for the VIP package to use it), but be prepared to tuck yourself into a little corner. I suggest bringing your own mat. The gym has two mats (two??) & they never get cleaned. The training staff is very toxic & gossip about each other &clients. I have heard trainers point out clients & make comments about their lack of progress, how they are still overweight, etc. In the main area pins are broken, seats ripped, etc. People also will use equipment as a place to sit and rest (and text), so be prepared to wait for a machine. On my last visit (which is catalyst for me to stop attending this gym) I heard a trainer say that I was a ‚Äústay-at-home type‚Äù who was making little progress. When I came in to notify my intent to cancel, I did so per the contract‚Äôs instructions, 30 days prior to the end. If you cancel be prepared for backlash! When you give your intent to cancel you‚Äôre met with rude staff that is unwilling to walk you through the process. You will have to meet with Denise to cancel personal training sessions (if you enrolled), filling out a form that states why your are cancelling. You will not get a copy of this form. I wasn‚Äôt given any paperwork notifying my intent to cancel, but was told they would ‚Äúcall me.‚Äù I still have time on my contract, so I went to Joe Bustamante to request info on cancellation. He was very rude and escalated the situation by responding aggressively and was very dismissive. He then said I needed to speak with someone named Jenelle and that she wasn‚Äôt there. In short, you cannot cancel until 30 days prior to your final month. If you do not cancel they will charge you each month until you cancel. After reviewing my contract, I realized that my credit card on file was about  to expire. Knowing that I needed to finish paying for the remainder of my contract I brought this up and was told I needed to speak with Denise, again, who was not available, and was told I would need to wait or come back. When I stated that I would wait Joe tried to get me to leave the gym, and stated that he would email me. I declined and said I would wait. An hour later when Denise was available I explained that I needed to update my card information. She shared that Joe & another front desk attendant named Randall could do that. (Seriously?!) I requested an email copy of my contract and Joe refused. He stated my physical copy was the same and that I didn‚Äôt need it. I pressed and was finally given a copy. Randall updated my payment info, when I said thank you for assisting he was rude in return and asked me to leave. (Even though I am still paying member.) <Review>We had some trouble with our AC the beginning of June and I called Shaw's and they immediately sent out a tech.  He took care of the problem.  Weather was cool, so we did not use the AC immediately.  We then started the AC and it began blowing cool air, but not enough to bring down our AC lower than 83 degrees.  I contacted Shaw's after hours and they immediately came out to figure out what the problem was.  It turns out that our AC was not blowing sufficient cool air to take bring down our AC from 85 degrees.   While we were trying to decide what action to take, one night I woke up during the night because I smelled something burning.  My husband went outside to make sure that our AC was not on fire.  Turns out that our AC had finally gave out.  Our house was at 89 degrees inside and Shaw's came out and brought us a portable unit to use for free.  Luckily we had a service contract, so we only had to pay the regular service charge (no OT).  Every time thereafter we did not have to pay a service charge until they were able to figure out what the problem was.
Shaw's gave us an estimate, which included a new AC unit, new Duct work (orig duct work 1976), larger Air Vents (that allow more air to flow), Return Air Filter (sucks up the hot air and allows the circulation of cool air to flow) and the installation of a new Thermostat, Carbon Monoxide sensor/alarm, and Fire Alarms in all 3 bedrooms.  We also received 10 year Warranty on parts and labor, 2 year service plan.  They disposed of the old unit and all of the old ductwork, including the old unit.  Last time we had the AC replaced, we had to pay for the disposal of the unit.  Once installed (87 degrees inside/ 102 outside) it took the unit an hour to come down to 80 degrees.
